			377 = {

					check_variable = { senator_1 = 1 }

					}
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = USA_Hardline_Republican_Goldwater_Leadership

						check_variable = { senator_1 = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}

	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = GetAlabamaSeat1Change
	text = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { 367.prev_senator_1 = 367.senator_1 }
		}
		localization_key = USA_alabama_seat_1_no_change
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { 367.senator_1 < 3 }
					check_variable = { 367.prev_senator_1 < 3 }
					NOT = {
						check_variable = { 367.prev_senator_1 = 367.senator_1 }
					}
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = { 367.senator_1 > 2 }
					check_variable = { 367.prev_senator_1 > 2 }
					NOT = {
						check_variable = { 367.prev_senator_1 = 367.senator_1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = USA_alabama_seat_1_change_primaried
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { 367.senator_1 < 3 }
					check_variable = { 367.prev_senator_1 > 2 }
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = { 367.senator_1 > 2 }
					check_variable = { 367.prev_senator_1 < 3 }
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = USA_alabama_seat_1_change
	}
}

					}
				}
			}

			check_variable = { 951.USA_recalled_prev_senator_1 = 951.USA_recalled_senator_1 }
		}
		localization_key = USA_new_hampshire_seat_1_no_change_prev
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { 951.USA_recalled_senator_1 < 3 }
					check_variable = { 951.USA_recalled_prev_senator_1 < 3 }
					NOT = {
						check_variable = { 951.USA_recalled_prev_senator_1 = 951.USA_recalled_senator_1 }
					}
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = { 951.USA_recalled_senator_1 > 2 }
					check_variable = { 951.USA_recalled_prev_senator_1 > 2 }
					NOT = {
						check_variable = { 951.USA_recalled_prev_senator_1 = 951.USA_recalled_senator_1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = USA_new_hampshire_seat_1_change_primaried_prev
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { 951.USA_recalled_senator_1 < 3 }
					check_variable = { 951.USA_recalled_prev_senator_1 > 2 }
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = { 951.USA_recalled_senator_1 > 2 }
					check_variable = { 951.USA_recalled_prev_senator_1 < 3 }
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = USA_new_hampshire_seat_1_change_prev
	}
}

		localization_key = USA_wyoming_seat_2_change_primaried_prev
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { 381.USA_recalled_senator_2 < 3 }
					check_variable = { 381.USA_recalled_prev_senator_2 > 2 }
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = { 381.USA_recalled_senator_2 > 2 }
					check_variable = { 381.USA_recalled_prev_senator_2 < 3 }
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = USA_wyoming_seat_2_change_prev
	}
}

#Alabama# #367#
defined_text = {
	name = GetAlabamaSeat1ChangePrediction
	text = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { 367.senate_seat_1_seatwarmer = 367.senator_1 }
		}
		localization_key = USA_alabama_seat_1_no_change_predictions
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { 367.senator_1 < 3 }
					check_variable = { 367.senate_seat_1_seatwarmer < 3 }
					NOT = {
						check_variable = { 367.senate_seat_1_seatwarmer = 367.senator_1 }
					}
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = { 367.senator_1 > 2 }
					check_variable = { 367.senate_seat_1_seatwarmer > 2 }
					NOT = {
						check_variable = { 367.senate_seat_1_seatwarmer = 367.senator_1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = USA_alabama_seat_1_change_primaried_prediction
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { 367.senator_1 < 3 }
					check_variable = { 367.senate_seat_1_seatwarmer > 2 }
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = { 367.senator_1 > 2 }
					check_variable = { 367.senate_seat_1_seatwarmer < 3 }
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = USA_alabama_seat_1_change_predictions
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = GetWhichDifferenceToDisplayRep
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_senate_elections
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_senate_conclusion
			}
			check_variable = { USA_GUI_selected_tab_sub = 1 }
		}
		localization_key = US_VOTE_REP_PRED
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_senate_elections
			has_country_flag = USA_senate_conclusion
			check_variable = { USA_GUI_selected_tab_sub = 1 }
